add_namespace = fate_of_ABA
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_ABA.0
	title = fate_of_ABA.0.t
	desc = fate_of_ABA.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABA.0.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = ABA	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ABA
					release_country_setting = yes
				}
			}
			else = {	ABA = {	release_country_setting = yes	}	}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_ABA.1
	title = fate_of_ABA.1.t
	desc = fate_of_ABA.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABA.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		country_event = fate_of_ABA.2
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_ABA.2
	title = fate_of_ABA.2.t
	desc = fate_of_ABA.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABA.2.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = ABA_republic_flag	}
		country_event = fate_of_ABA.0
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABA.2.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AMERICA_confederate_states_flag	}
		country_event = fate_of_ABA.0
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABA.2.2
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AMERICA_united_states_flag	}
		country_event = fate_of_ABA.0
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.3
	title = fate_of_AFG.3.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.3.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		country_event = fate_of_AFG.0
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.3.1
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	STR_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {	
				any_owned_state = {
					check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
					check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
				}
			}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.3.2
		ROOT = {	
			set_country_flag = AFG_STR_region_flag
			set_country_flag = AFG_all_BAL_region_flag
			set_country_flag = AFG_all_PAK_region_flag
			set_country_flag = AFG_all_KAS_region_flag
		}
		country_event = fate_of_AFG.0
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.4
	title = fate_of_AFG.4.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.4.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.4.0
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	STR_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		if = {
			limit = {	
				any_owned_state = {
					check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
					check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
				}
			}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.4.1
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	STR_state_variable = 1	}
			}
			any_owned_state = {
				check_variable = {	STR_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	TAJ_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_STR_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	
				any_owned_state = {
					check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
					check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
				}
			}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.4.2
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_not_STR_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	
				any_owned_state = {
					check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
					check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
				}
			}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	STR_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_STR.1
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.5
	title = fate_of_AFG.5.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.5.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.5.0
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.5.1
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_western_BAL_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.5.2
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
			any_owned_state = {	
				check_variable = {	PER_state_variable = 1	}
				check_variable = {	BAL_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_all_BAL_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.5.3
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_not_BAL_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.6
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.6
	title = fate_of_AFG.6.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.6.0
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_PASHTUNISTAN_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	KAS_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.7
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.6.1
		trigger = {
			any_owned_state = {
				NOT ={	check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 2	}	}
				check_variable = {	PAK_state_variable = 1	}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = AFG_all_PAK_region_flag	}
		if = {
			limit = {	any_owned_state = {	check_variable = {	KAS_state_variable = 1	}	}	}
			country_event = fate_of_AFG.7
		}
		else = {	country_event = fate_of_AFG.0	}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.6.2
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		country_event = fate_of_AFG.0
	}
}

	title = fate_of_GAN.0.t
	desc = fate_of_GAN.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_GAN.0.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = GAN	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = GAN
					release_country_setting = yes
				}
			}
			else = {	GAN = {	release_country_setting = yes	}	}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_GAN.1
	title = fate_of_GAN.1.t

	option = {

	title = fate_of_LIE.2.t
	desc = fate_of_LIE.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_LIE.2.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		ROOT = {	set_country_flag = LIE_republic_flag	}
		country_event = fate_of_LIE.0
	}
}
	
add_namespace = fate_of_LIT
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_LIT.0
	title = fate_of_LIT.0.t
	desc = fate_of_LIT.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_LIT.0.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = LIT	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = LIT
					release_country_setting = yes
				}
			}
			else = {	LIT = {	release_country_setting = yes	}	}
		}
	}
}

	title = fate_of_MYT.1.t
	desc = fate_of_MYT.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = fate_of_MYT.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		country_event = fate_of_MYT.2
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_MYT.2
	title = fate_of_MYT.2.t
	desc = fate_of_MYT.2.d

	option = {

add_namespace = fate_of_MZB
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_MZB.0
	title = fate_of_MZB.0.t
	desc = fate_of_MZB.0.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_MZB.0.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = MZB	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = MZB
					release_country_setting = yes
				}
			}
			else = {	MZB = {	release_country_setting = yes	}	}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ZAN.0.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = ZAN	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ZAN
					release_country_setting = yes
				}
			}
			else = {	ZAN = {	release_country_setting = yes	}	}
		}
	}
}
